Hi Esther,
We hope you've had an amazing stay at Serenity Cabin and that the accommodations have exceeded your expectations.

We know accidents happen - if there are any accidental damages or issues, please reply back or give us a call so we can address the issues before our incoming guests. Your security deposit will be refunded after we have done a walk through of the home (funds can take up to 5-10 days to reflect in your account).

Here are your checkout instructions:
1.Check-out time is at 11:00. To ensure we have time to prepare for our incoming guests, please be prepared to leave on time. Our cleaners will need to access the property to sanitize and prepare the home.
2. Please lock all windows and doors upon departure
3. Wash any dishes and start dishwasher
4. Leave any dirty towels in the bathtubs/showers
5. No need to strip the beds - our cleaners will take care of those for you!
6. Remove all trash from the property and dispose in the garbage bins
7. Check throughout the house (including under the beds, in drawers, and around all electrical outlets) for any personal items.
8. Turn off all lights
9. If you've moved any furniture or belongings, please put them back in their original places.
10. Sign our guest book - we'd love to hear about your favorite memory made at Serenity Cabin.

Thank you so much for choosing Serenity Cabin! We hope you'll leave a positive review and will come back soon!

Safe travels,
Serenity Cabins

Received via Vrbo on Tuesday, November 18th, 2025 at 10:51 AM

Hello Joe,

We have confirmed that a refund was already in progress when you chose to initiate a credit card chargeback. Because the chargeback supersedes our internal process, we are now required to treat this as a potential fraud case under our policies and turn the matter over to the bank for resolution. This will cause a delay in the release of any funds, particularly given the timing with our end-of-month bookkeeping.

Please note that by filing a chargeback while a refund was underway, you may have forfeited the courtesy refund we initiated. If the bank determines the chargeback is invalid, we reserve the right to enforce our cancellation policy in full.

At this stage, you will need to work directly with your credit card company regarding the dispute. We also strongly recommend you engage your travel insurance provider, as they are often best positioned to assist with covered disruptions or losses.

We will abide by the outcome of the bank’s process, but we cannot take further action on your behalf while the dispute is active.

Sincerely,
James
Serenity Cabins

Hi Rhonda,
We hope you've had an amazing stay at Woodward Cottage and that the accommodations have exceeded your expectations.

We know accidents happen - if there are any accidental damages or issues, please reply back or give us a call so we can address the issues before our incoming guests. Your security deposit will be refunded after we have done a walk through of the home (funds can take up to 5-10 days to reflect in your account).

Here are your checkout instructions:
1.Check-out time is at 11:00. To ensure we have time to prepare for our incoming guests, please be prepared to leave on time. Our cleaners will need to access the property to sanitize and prepare the home.
2. Please lock all windows and doors upon departure
3. Wash any dishes and start dishwasher
4. Leave any dirty towels in the bathtubs/showers
5. No need to strip the beds - our cleaners will take care of those for you!
6. Remove all trash from the property and dispose in the garbage bins
7. Check throughout the house (including under the beds, in drawers, and around all electrical outlets) for any personal items.
8. Turn off all lights
9. If you've moved any furniture or belongings, please put them back in their original places.
10. Sign our guest book - we'd love to hear about your favorite memory made at Woodward Cottage.

Thank you so much for choosing Woodward Cottage! We hope you'll leave a positive review and will come back soon!

Safe travels,
Serenity Cabins

Hello Molly, 

Here is a list of our local recommendations:

Upperville (~3 min):

Hunter’s Head Tavern - old style pub with a great patio; can be hard to get a reservation, but it’s just a few mins drive from the house and they do takeout 
Market at Bluewater Kitchen - gourmet sandwiches and salads in Upperville 
Slaterrun Vineyards - family-run vineyard specializing in French-style wine; reservations are recommended for 21+ (no pets are allowed)

Middleburg (~10 min):

Knead Wine - artisanal pizza and wine for takeout 
Tremolo - excellent high-end wine bar (with the same owner as Knead Wine)
Thaiverse - good for Thai takeout and has a lovely patio for dining
Lost Barrel Brewery - a fun brewery between the house and Middleburg; you can rent a firepit and order food from their menu, and kids are allowed 

Delaplane (~12 min, past Upperville off Route 50):

Sky Meadows State Park - lots of good hiking trails, some challenging and some easy

Marshall (~17 min):

Red Truck Bakery - a good bakery in Marshall 
Field & Main - upscale restaurant with indoor seating and cabanas for private seatings

The Plains (~20 min, near Marshall):

Archwood Green Barns Farmers’ Market - this market is about 20 mins from the house; it’s open on Sundays from 10am-2pm (but confirm the hours online)

Bluemont (~20 min):

Dirt Farm Brewery - brewery in Bluemont with excellent views next to Bluemont Vineyard and Great Country Farms; kids are allowed
Great Country Farms - farm with seasonal “festivals” and pumpkin picking; can get mobbed during fall weekends but kids enjoy the ninja course and slides, along with the cider donuts; buy tickets online

Aldie (~20 min):

Gilbert’s Corner farmers’ market - this market is in Aldie on Route 50; the French bakery is good and they often have a fresh donut stand, oysters, barbecue, coffee, ice cream, etc.
Aldie Peddler - this is a good spot to pick up wine and honey

Round Hill (~23 min, near Bluemont):

More Better Restaurant & Beer Garden - good spot for brunch or lunch, with both indoor and outdoor tables; they don't take reservations 
Mom’s Apple Pie - the location in Round Hill (it’s next to More Better) has all kinds of pies and other desserts; they also have wine and beer

Linden (~30 min):

Linden Vineyards - great wine and views; they take reservations and are 21+

Pool Operation: To operate the pool cover please use the key on the far side of the pool house. Look carefully for the mailbox marked 1327; it is easy to miss on your first time visiting.Then turn into the gravel driveway and through the gates marked LV.Proceed straight on the gravel driveway past the main house.You will see a fence with a gate; feel free to park here.To open the lockbox, enter the code 7231. Use the key to unlock the door that it is hanging from.Be careful not to lose the key to avoid a replacement fee.Also, be careful not to accidentally engage the lock. It can automatically lock, leaving you stranded outside!

Thank you for staying with us and safe travels,
Serenity Cabins

3. Wash any dishes and start dishwasher
4. Leave any dirty towels in the bathtubs/showers
5. No need to strip the beds - our cleaners will take care of those for you!
6. Remove all trash from the property and dispose in the garbage bins
7. Check throughout the house (including under the beds, in drawers, and around all electrical outlets) for any personal items.
8. Turn off all lights
9. If you've moved any furniture or belongings, please put them back in their original places.
10. Sign our guest book - we'd love to hear about your favorite memory made at The Clover House Georgetown.

Thank you so much for choosing The Clover House Georgetown! We hope you'll leave a positive review and will come back soon!

Serenity Cabins
